handles token auto-mounting for pods. The plugin implements two key decision functions:\\n\\n1. **shouldAutomount()** (line 254): This function determines whether a service account token should be mounted based on precedence rules:\\n   - First checks pod.Spec.AutomountServiceAccountToken (Pod-level setting wins)\\n   - Falls back to serviceAccount.AutomountServiceAccountToken (ServiceAccount-level setting)\\n   - Defaults to true for backward compatibility\\n\\n2. **mountServiceAccountToken()** (line 416): When automounting is enabled, this method:\\n   - Finds or generates a unique volume name with the prefix \\\"kube-api-access\\\"\\n   - Adds a VolumeMount to all containers pointing to /var/run/secrets/kubernetes.io/serviceaccount\\n   - Injects a projected volume containing the service account token\\n\\n3. **TokenVolumeSource()** (line 485): Returns a ProjectedVolumeSource containing:\\n   - A ServiceAccountTokenProjection with the token at path \\\"token\\\"\\n   - A ConfigMapProjection for the \\\"kube-root-ca.crt\\\" root CA certificate\\n   - The token uses the WarnOnlyBoundTokenExpirationSeconds expiration setting\\n\\nThe admission controller is registered with the name \\\"ServiceAccount\\\" and processes both Pod CREATE and UPDATE operations.\\n\\n## Token Controller (Secret Creation)\\nThe token controller at `pkg/controller/serviceaccount/tokens_controller.go` creates and manages the actual token secrets:\\n\\n1. **TokensController** is initialized by `NewTokensController()` (line 74) with:\\n   - A TokenGenerator for creating signed JWT tokens\\n   - Service account and secret informers for tracking changes\\n   - Work queues for asynchronous processing\\n\\n2. The controller watches ServiceAccount objects and creates corresponding SecretTypeServiceAccountToken secrets containing:\\n   - The token data (signed JWT)\\n   - Annotations linking to the ServiceAccount (name and UID)\\n   - The root CA certificate\\n\\n## Token Generation\\nThe `pkg/serviceaccount/jwt.go` file provides:\\n\\n1. **JWTTokenGenerator()** (line 61): Creates a TokenGenerator that signs tokens using RSA or ECDSA private keys\\n2. **TokenGenerator interface**: Defines the contract for token generation\\n\\n## Service Account Token Controller Setup\\nThe `cmd/kube-controller-manager/app/service_accounts.go` orchestrates initialization:\\n\\n1. **newServiceAccountTokenControllerDescriptor()** (line 33): Creates a ControllerDescriptor marked as requiring special handling (started first before other controllers)\\n\\n2. **newServiceAccountTokenController()** (line 45): Initializes the TokensController by:\\n   - Reading the service account signing private key file\\n   - Reading the root CA certificate\\n   - Creating a JWTTokenGenerator\\n   - Instantiating the TokensController with these components\\n\\n## Pod Spec Validation\\nThe AutomountServiceAccountToken field is defined in:\\n- `pkg/apis/core/types.go` (PodSpec at line 3734, ServiceAccount at line 5326)\\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/api/core/v1/types.go` (the v1 API version definitions)\\n\\nThis boolean field (when set) overrides the default behavior and allows users to explicitly disable token mounting for specific pods or service accounts.\\n\\n## Supporting
